<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">декор(и́ровать)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dekor(írovatʹ)</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́тор</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átor</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, or borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">decorator</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:декоратор.html>декора́тор</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dekorátor</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:декоратор.html>декора́тора</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:декоратор.html>декора́торы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:декоратор.html>декора́торов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>decorator</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:декрет.html>декре́т</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dekrét</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:декрет.html>декре́та</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:декрет.html>декре́ты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:декрет.html>декре́тов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>decree, edict</li>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:де.html>де́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:лан.html>лан</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ный</b>
</p><p>Страдательное <a href = vnd.unilang:причастие.html>прича́стие</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:прошедший.html>проше́дшего</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:время.html>вре́мени</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1*a(2).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-дел-</b>; суффиксы: <b>-а-нн</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ый</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
</p>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:де.html>де́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>лать</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:сделать.html>сде́лать</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-дел-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
</p>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:делать.html>де́лать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">délatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:делаться.html>де́латься</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">délatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сделаться.html>сде́латься</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to become, to get, to grow, to turn
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:делаться.html>де́лается</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:темный.html>темно́</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Délajetsja</b> temnó.</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>It is getting</b> dark. / <b>It is growing</b> dark.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to happen (with, to), to be going on
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>Что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:там.html>там</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:делаться.html>де́лается</a></b>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Što tam <b>délajetsja</b>?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">What <b>is going on</b> there?</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:делать.html>де́лать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">délatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:деликатес.html>деликате́с</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">delikatɛ́s</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:деликатес.html>деликате́са</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:деликатес.html>деликате́сы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:деликатес.html>деликате́сов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>delicacy; dainty; delicatessen; tidbit; gourmet food</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:деликатность.html>делика́тность</a> (14165)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:деликатный.html>делика́тный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">delikátnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ость</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:деликатность.html>делика́тность</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">delikátnostʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:деликатность.html>делика́тности</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:деликатность.html>делика́тности</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:деликатность.html>делика́тностей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>tact, tactfulness, delicacy</li></ol>

***деликатный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:деликатный.html>делика́тный</a> (8541)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">delikat</i> + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:деликатный.html>делика́тный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">delikátnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)делика́тнее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)делика́тней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>delicate, considerate, tactful</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> subtle, fragile, delicate</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> delicate, sensitive, ticklish</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">polite</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воспитать.html>воспи́танный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vospítannyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">tactful</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тактичный.html>такти́чный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">taktíčnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***делить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:делить.html>дели́ть</a> (4509)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*děliti</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to divide</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Balto-Slavic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Balto-Slavic language">Proto-Balto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-bsl-pro">*doyl-</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*dʰayl-</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*dʰoyl-</i>. Cognates include <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">dǣlan</i> (<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">deal</i>) and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lithuanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Lithuanian language">Lithuanian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt">dailyti</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:делить.html>дели́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">delítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поделить.html>подели́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разделить.html>раздели́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to divide</li>
<li>to share, to exchange</li>
<li>to confide, to tell</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разделять.html>разделя́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">razdeljátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разъединять.html>разъединя́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">razʺjedinjátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">расчленя́ть</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">rasčlenjátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разнимать.html>разнима́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">raznimátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 4c[④]⑦.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́лы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:поделить.html>подели́ть</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:разделить.html>раздели́ть</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-дел-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:соорудить.html>-и</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b>. <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:делить.html>дели́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">delítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:делиться.html>дели́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">delítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поделиться.html>подели́ться</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разделиться.html>раздели́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:делить.html>дели́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">delítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li>
<li>to be divided</li>
<li>to be divisible (only imperfective)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пять.html>пять</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>два</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:делиться.html>де́лится</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pjatʹ na dva ne <b>délitsja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">five is not divisible by two</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to share (perfective: <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поделиться.html>подели́ться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">podelítʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:делиться.html>дели́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:кусок.html>куско́м</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:хлеб.html>хле́ба</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>delítʹsja</b> kuskóm xléba</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to share a piece of bread, (fig.) to share meals with somebody</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:делиться.html>дели́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:впечатление.html>впечатле́ниями</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>delítʹsja</b> vpečatlénijami</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to share one's impressions</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:де.html>де</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:лить.html>ли́ть</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ся</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,  <a href = vnd.unilang:возвратный.html>возвра́тный</a>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 4c.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́лы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:разделиться.html>раздели́ться</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:поделиться.html>подели́ться</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-дел-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:соорудить.html>-и</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b>; постфикс: <b>-ся</b>.
</p>

***дело.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дело.html>дело</a> (67)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*dělo</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*děti</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*dʰeh₁-</i>, whence English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">deed</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">fact</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">affair</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дело.html>де́ло</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">délo</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дело.html>де́ла</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дело.html>дела́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дело.html>де́л</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>affair, matter, concern
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:министерство.html>министе́рство</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:иностранный.html>иностра́нных</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:дело.html>де́л</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ministérstvo inostránnyx <b>del</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">Ministry of Foreign <b>Affairs</b></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>У</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>меня́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сложиться.html>сложи́лась</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:картина.html>карти́на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:основной.html>основны́х</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:факт.html>фа́ктов</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́тому</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:дело.html>де́лу</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">U menjá složílasʹ kartína osnovnýx fáktov po étomu <b>délu</b>.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I have a grip of the essential facts of this case.</span></dd><dd>(literally, “<span class="e-literally">A picture of core facts to this <b>case</b> took shape for me.</span>”)</dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>work, business
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>Как</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:дело.html>дела́</a></b>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Kak <b>delá</b>?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">How are you? (informal)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>Как</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:дело.html>дела́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:идти.html>иду́т</a>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Kak <b>delá</b> idút?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">How are you? (formal)</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>art, science
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:золотой.html>золоты́х</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:дело.html>де́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мастер.html>ма́стер</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">zolotýx <b>del</b> máster</i> ― <span class="e-translation">a master goldsmith</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">a master of the golden arts</span>”)</div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:горный.html>го́рное</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:дело.html>де́ло</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">górnoje <b>délo</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">mining</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">mountain science</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li>
<li>deed, act, action</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">law</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> case, investigation
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>На</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>него́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:заведённый.html>заведено́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:уголовный.html>уголо́вное</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:дело.html>де́ло</a></b>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Na nevó zavedenó ugolóvnoje <b>délo</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">He is the subject of a criminal <b>case</b>.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">law enforcement</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> file, dossier
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выписка.html>вы́писка</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:личный.html>ли́чного</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:дело.html>де́ла</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">výpiska iz jevó líčnovo <b>déla</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">a copy of a page from his police <b>file</b></span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>cause

<li><i>in expressions</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>Не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:дело.html>де́ло</a></b>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ne <b>délo</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">That's not a good idea.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:но.html>Но</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:дело.html>де́ло</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:даже.html>да́же</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́том</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">No <b>délo</b> dáže ne v étom.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">It's not even that. / That's not even what the problem is.</span></div></dd>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:де.html>де́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ло</b> (<span title="написание в дореформенной орфографии" style="border-bottom: 1px dotted; cursor: help">дореформ.</span> <span style="font-family: | Palatino Linotype | ">дѣло</span>)
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:средний.html>сре́дний</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 2-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 1c  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка) |  <a href = vnd.unilang:встречаться.html>встреча́ется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>также</a> нарочито-сниж. <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:простой.html>прост</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:форма.html>фо́рма</a> рд. мн.: <i>дело́в</i>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-дел-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-о</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-де-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:смекалка.html>-л</a></b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-о</b>  | Кузнецова, Ефремова, 1986 | .

***деловой.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:деловой.html>делово́й</a> (2493)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дело.html>де́ло</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">délo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ово́й</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:деловой.html>делово́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">delovój</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> business, work, working
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:деловой.html>деловы́е</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:круг.html>круги́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>delovýje</b> krugí</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>business</b> community, <b>business</b> interest</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>businesslike</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дельный.html>де́льный</a> (14629)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дело.html>де́ло</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">délo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дельный.html>де́льный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">délʹnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)дельне́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)дельне́й</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>efficient, businesslike
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:дельный.html>де́льный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>челове́к</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>délʹnyj</b> čelovék</i> ― <span class="e-translation">able person</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>sensible
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:дельный.html>де́льный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:разговор.html>разгово́р</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>délʹnyj</b> razgovór</i> ― <span class="e-translation">productive talk/conversation</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:дельный.html>де́льный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:совет.html>сове́т</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>délʹnyj</b> sovét</i> ― <span class="e-translation">useful advice</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:дельный.html>де́льное</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:предложение.html>предложе́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>délʹnoje</b> predložénije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">sensible suggestion</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дельта.html>де́льта</a> (18127)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">δέλτα</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">délta</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, whereas the sense of a deltoid is a clipping of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">дельтови́дная <a href = vnd.unilang:мышца.html>мы́шца</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">delʹtovídnaja mýšca</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***делянка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:делянка.html>деля́нка</a> (26199)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">деля́на</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">deljána</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">plot of land for cultivation</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:делить.html>дели́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">delítʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to divide</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:делянка.html>деля́нка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">deljánka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:делянка.html>деля́нки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:делянка.html>деля́нки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:делянка.html>деля́нок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>plot of land for cultivation or cutting down</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">regional</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> share, portion</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> share of total work allocated to someone</li></ol>

***демобилизация.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:демобилизация.html>демобилиза́ция</a> (24122)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">démobilisation</i>.
